| <span data-ttu-id="a8029-936">進入</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a8029-936">Entry</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a8029-937">值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a8029-937">Value</span></span> |
